# Comments for Question 1, LLM=Llama 4 Maverick

== Grader: Claude 3.7 Sonnet ==
  * grade_story_101.txt (grade=4.2)
    Emma lacks depth beyond her role as a guardian of creative space. Her motivation to help others "reimagine endings" is stated repeatedly but never demonstrated through specific actions or personal history. The character remains a vague archetype rather than a fully realized individual with complexities or contradictions. Her reaction to the napoleonic bee pin feels superficial rather than revealing genuine character insight.

  * grade_story_100.txt (grade=5.2)
    The "vivid dreamer" character lacks depth beyond their basic motivation. While their "rationally mischievous" attribute appears in their grin, it doesn't meaningfully shape their actions. Their relationship with the pressed penny collection is mentioned but not explored in a way that reveals character. The character remains largely a vessel for experiencing the setting rather than a fully realized individual with agency.

  * grade_story_1.txt (grade=5.2)
    The character's phobia-ridden nature is established early but lacks specificity—we never learn what actual phobias plague them. The stunt double aspect is mentioned only once near the end and feels tacked on rather than integral to identity. Their motivation to "dance on the edge of madness" is stated but not demonstrated through meaningful choices. The character's voice remains generic throughout, with emotional states told rather than shown through distinctive perspective.

  * grade_story_10.txt (grade=5.2)
    The duelist's motivation to learn forgiveness through cooking is intriguing but underdeveloped. Their character lacks specificity—we know they're cheerless and seeking redemption, but their personality remains generic. The connection between dueling, cooking, and forgiveness feels forced rather than organic to the character. Their internal journey lacks nuanced progression, relying on telling rather than showing their transformation.

  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=5.2)
    The spy's "sheepish" and "analytically creative" traits are established but not deeply explored. Their motivation to charm the monster and unite factions is clear, but their personality lacks distinctive depth. The character remains somewhat generic despite having assigned traits—we see what they do but get limited insight into who they truly are beyond their mission.

  * grade_story_11.txt (grade=5.2)
    The "flighty cartographer" trait is established but not deeply explored. Her methodical approach contradicts her supposed flightiness. The "serene anger" motivation feels underdeveloped and contradictory. While we understand she wants to leave a legacy, her personality lacks distinctive voice and emotional depth beyond surface-level description.

  * grade_story_104.txt (grade=6.8)
    The stoic steward is consistently characterized through their careful, reverent handling of artifacts and their quiet rebellion against conformity. Their motivation to preserve uniqueness is clear, though their personal history and deeper emotional complexity remain undeveloped. The character's actions align well with their established traits, but the lack of dialogue or more varied emotional responses limits their dimensionality.

  * grade_story_108.txt (grade=5.2)
    The minstrel's vexed nature and strategic spontaneity are mentioned but not deeply explored. His motivation to calm the crowd is stated directly rather than revealed through action. The character lacks distinctive voice or dialogue that would make him memorable, and his relationship with the spy pen remains functional rather than revealing deeper character traits.

  * grade_story_103.txt (grade=6.2)

His reactions to the pattern and reflection feel somewhat generic rather than revealing unique aspects of his character.

  * grade_story_105.txt (grade=5.2)
